02:15:08","updatedTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","title":"Cruise lines and Florida are on track for a standoff over COVID-19 vaccine requirements","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/cruise-lines-florida-conflict-covid-vaccine-requirements-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6075c2c33e3fe7001882a61c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"carnival cruise\" height=\"1333\" width=\"1778\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Carnival Ecstasy docked at the Port of Jacksonville on March 27, 2020 in Jacksonville, Florida.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Sam Greenwood/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Florida Gov. Ron DeSantis&#39; executive order banning businesses from requiring vaccines applies to cruise lines.</li>\n<li>However, several cruise lines have already announced vaccine mandates.</li>\n<li>DeSantis has been vocal about the cruise industry and previously said the state would sue the CDC to bring cruises back sooner.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Florida and cruise companies could be locked in a battle over vaccine requirements as the state puts a ban on vaccine passports while cruise lines continue to mandate the jabs for passengers and crew.</p><p>On April 2, Florida Gov. Ron DeSantis<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/desantis-florida-vaccine-passport-ban2021-4\"> issued an executive order</a> banning vaccine passports and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/kayak-first-hotel-in-miami-beach-florida-tech-life-house-2021-3\">local businesses</a> from requiring this proof of vaccination. This ban applies to cruise lines as well, DeSantis&#39; press secretary Cody McCloud told Insider in an email.</p><p>&#34;The Governor&#39;s Executive Order provides that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/travelers-are-flocking-to-miami-for-spring-break-despite-covid-2021-3\">businesses in Florida </a>are prohibited from requiring patrons or customers to provide any documentation certifying COVID-19 vaccination or post-transmission recovery to gain access to, entry upon, or service from the business,&#34; McCloud told Insider in an email. &#34;Therefore, the Executive Order prohibits cruise lines from requiring vaccine passports for their Florida operations.&#34;</p><p><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-south-florida-became-the-conservative-shadow-capital-2021-4\">The Great GOP Migration: How South Florida became a shadow capital for Trump conservatives</a></em></p><p>However, many cruise lines have already <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cruise-ship-covid-vaccine-requirements-guests-crew-each-company-2021-2\">announced some form of a vaccine requirement</a>, whether it be for crew, guests, or both. This includes Norwegian Cruise Line Holdings, which <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/norwegian-cruise-line-requiring-covid-vaccine-for-guests-crew-on-new-cruises-2021-4\">recently unveiled a sweeping vaccine requirement</a> for its Norwegian, Oceania, and Regent Seven Seas brand. Other cruise lines, such as Royal Caribbean, have held off on guest or crew requirements, instead opting to announce<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/social-media-facebok-twitter-for-royal-caribbean-cruise-boycott-2021-3\"> select &#34;fully vaccinated&#34; sailings</a>.</p><p>However, major cruise lines - with the exception of those with a sweeping vaccine mandate - have withheld announcing a vaccine policy for future sailing series departing from US ports. So far, all of Royal Caribbean&#39;s cruises operating under a vaccine order will be sailing out of international ports located in countries like Israel, Bermuda, and Cyprus. </p><p>DeSantis&#39; decision to prohibit cruise lines from requiring vaccines could prove to be yet another major issue for cruise companies, many of which have historically sailed out of Florida ports. But some experts have questioned DeSantis&#39; <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/miami-beach-extended-state-of-emergency-spring-break-travelers-2021-3\">ability to impose such a ban upon cruise lines</a>, according to a <a href=\"https://www.sun-sentinel.com/business/fl-bz-silversea-cruises-to-require-vaccinations-20210412-7ok6fwabpndc5aop6oyla5tgvq-story.html\">report from the Sun Sentinel</a>.</p><p>This includes Jim Walker - an attorney based in South Florida with a specialization in maritime law - who told the <a href=\"https://www.sun-sentinel.com/business/fl-bz-silversea-cruises-to-require-vaccinations-20210412-7ok6fwabpndc5aop6oyla5tgvq-story.html\">Sun Sentinel</a> that DeSantis may not have the jurisdiction needed to either prohibit cruise lines from enforcing a vaccine mandate or<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/florida-sue-cdc-cruise-industry-pause-2021-4\"> bring cruises back</a>. </p><p>Regardless, it could be a while before we see any stand-off between the state and cruise lines interested in sailing out of Florida with a vaccine requirement.</p><p>The US Centers for Disease Control and Prevention has yet to give cruise lines the green light to resume sailing and has <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cruises-safest-place-on-earth-covid-vaccine-norwegian-cruise-ceo-2021-4\">shied away from enforcing an industry-wide vaccine mandate</a>. As a result, no major cruise lines will be sailing from US ports in the near future, even if the ship is traveling with a vaccine mandate.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on Masthead Sticky</bi-shortcode><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>An indoor antenna allows you to watch free local channels on your TV without a cable plan.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\">Modern antennas can be attached to your wall or placed on a stand for easy installation.</li>\n<li>Our top choice is the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0754WJ3FX/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=B0754WJ3FX&linkId=1cf6e73d174f1496a69487a468557d00174f1496a69487a468557d00\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Channel Master FLATenna+</a> thanks to its simple setup and strong reception.</li>\n</ul><p>An indoor antenna is a cheap and simple way to get local TV channels without a cable or streaming subscription</p><p>Most antennas today are as thin as a sheet of paper and can get dozens of channels as far as 60 miles away. You can tape some antennas right on your wall for easy setup. Others are as compact as a salt shaker, letting you easily place them behind your TV. </p><p>Instead of paying a hefty monthly bill, you can score a solid antenna for a one-time payment as little as $19. This affordable investment will get you free access to local stations like ABC, NBC, CBS, and Fox. But, before you pick up an antenna, you&#39;ll want to use the <a href=\"http://www.antennaweb.org/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">AntennaWeb tool</a> to see exactly what stations are available in your area. </p><p>Depending on whether you live in a big city or a more rural area with access to fewer channels, antennas may or may not be the right choice for you. You&#39;ll also want to consider what channels are exclusive to cable/streaming services versus what channels you might find with an antenna.</p><p>For most people, an antenna can be a cost-effective way to score live TV without a recurring cost. After testing several different models, we&#39;ve picked the best antennas you can buy, all for under $100.</p><h2>Here are the best indoor antennas of 2021:</h2><ul href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0754WJ3FX/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B0754WJ3FX&#38;linkId=1cf6e73d174f1496a69487a468557d00\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Channel Master FLATenna+</a> is a lightweight antenna with a wide range, reliable reception, and an affordable price.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>Design</strong>: Flat for wall or window</li><li><strong>Range</strong>: Up to 50 miles</li><li><strong>Amplifier</strong>: MicroAmp to improve signal</li><li><strong>Channels received</strong>: 70 during our testing</li></ul></aside><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Amplifier addresses choppy picture, subtle design, includes 3M tape for attaching to your wall, coaxial cable included</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Takes longer to install due to amplifier</p><p>Out of all the antennas we tested, the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0754WJ3FX/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B0754WJ3FX&#38;linkId=1cf6e73d174f1496a69487a468557d00\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Channel Master FLATenna+</a> offers the best bang for your buck. For $40, you get a reliable indoor antenna that's relatively easy to install and offers a range of around 50 miles.&#160;</p><p>The model is paper thin and you can stick it to any part of your wall or window after applying the included 3M tape to the back. After I hung up the antenna it firmly held itself to the wall for over four weeks while testing.</p><p>The downside is that it takes slightly longer to install, but that's due to Channel Master's MicroAmp that you can screw in to improve reception. Channel Master claims its MicroAmp helps receive difficult-to-reach channels and, while that may be true, it makes this model a little less plug-and-play friendly.&#160;</p><p>In my area, the antenna picked up eight 1080i channels, including CBS, NBC, ABC, Fox, government channels, and Telemundo. It also picked up 62 other local stations while eliminating a number of channels that appeared choppy on Channel Master's FLATenna 35 model.&#160;</p><p>In fact, none of the channels I watched with this antenna were choppy. It's a breeze to flip through stations and, over time, none of the channels disappeared from my lineup. When stacked up to other antennas we tested, this model also had shorter delays when picking up a station.</p><p>If you're looking for an affordable indoor antenna with a simple design and reliable reception, this one is your best bet overall.</p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Note:</strong> This item is expected to be back in stock on April 16.</p></aside>\n\tThe best budget indoor antenna\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064cabb6183e1001981994e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Channel Master’s FLATenna&#43; The main difference here is that this model does not include the MicroAmp or coaxial cable. We found that the MicroAmp helped provide better reception, but if you're on a budget, the base model is still a good buy.&#160;</p><p>Just like the FLATenna+, this model is paper thin and you just need the 3M tape included in the package to install it on a wall or window.&#160;Channel Master is currently including a 12-foot coaxial cable for free if you buy the antenna through its site, but this model doesn't usually come with a cable.</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B074TWSQFM/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B074TWSQFM&#38;linkId=54cf1593abf5798a85bb0212ab0dd71a\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">FLATenna 35</a> received my local ABC, NBC, CBS, and Fox channels. It also found a lot of Spanish language channels including Univision, Azteca, Estrela, and more. Other local stations, like Crime and GetTV, came through without any issues. I received 22 channels with a picture quality of 720p or higher.</p><p>Compared to other antennas I tested, the only major channel the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B074TWSQFM/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B074TWSQFM&#38;linkId=54cf1593abf5798a85bb0212ab0dd71a\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">FLATenna</a> couldn't pick up was PBS Kids. But while I received 79 channels, a handful of those stations came through with choppy images, which isn't ideal. Since it doesn't include the MicroAmp, this model is rated for a shorter range of 35 miles, which might account for the choppiness.&#160;</p>\n\tThe best indoor/outdoor combo antenna\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064cad56183e1001981994f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Antennas Direct’s ClearStream 2Max antenna\" height=\"788\" width=\"1051\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ben Blanchet/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1736470766984890722\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Antennas Direct ClearStream 2Max</a> features a solid, stable design that can be used indoors and outdoors.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>Design:</strong> Table top or wall mount, outdoor-ready</li><li><strong>Range:</strong> Up to 60 miles</li><li><strong>Amplifier: </strong>Not included</li><li><strong>Channels received:</strong> 65 during our testing</li></ul></aside><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Unique design, sturdy feel, solid channel reception, designed for indoor and outdoor use</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Pricey, difficult setup, no coaxial cord included</p><p>The <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1736470766984890722\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Antennas Direct ClearStream 2Max</a> stands out from other models with its interesting design as, once you lift it up, the antenna looks like a bird flying in the sky.&#160;</p><p>The setup takes roughly 10 minutes and, while it was difficult to put the mount on at the bottom, it remained sturdy throughout my use. There wasn't any choppy picture on any of the channels I tested, and it managed to receive all the major local offerings, such as ABC, NBC, CBS, and Fox.&#160;</p><p>While this model firmly stands on its own after setup, it's important to note that it doesn't come with a coaxial cable. This isn't a huge hassle, however, as coaxial cables are sold at many stores. But, the omission is still disappointing given the antenna's already high cost.</p><p>Although it's pricier than our other picks, this model has the added flexibility to be used outside instead of indoors if you want a better signal. The model's mounting base allows you to clamp the antenna onto your roof or home to capture signals outdoors.&#160;</p>\n\tThe best compact indoor antenna\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064bd87daf0f10018f9948e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Antennas Direct’s ClearStream Eclipse Amplified antenna\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ben Blanchet/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B01HZD5MUM/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B01HZD5MUM&#38;linkId=6a37a6d9f9d7086e4495bcb220ac1691\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Antennas Direct ClearStream Eclipse</a> is a thin amplified antenna that takes up little space.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>Design:</strong> Flat for wall or window</li><li><strong>Range: </strong>Up to 50 miles</li><li><strong>Amplifier:</strong> 15db Jolt in-line amplifier</li><li><strong>Channels received: </strong>56 during our testing</li></ul></aside><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Quick access to channels, thin and compact, coaxial cable included</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>PBS channels difficult to find in my area</p><p>Although the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B01HZD5MUM/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B01HZD5MUM&#38;linkId=6a37a6d9f9d7086e4495bcb220ac1691\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Antennas Direct ClearStream Eclipse Amplified</a> picked up about nine channels less than the 2Max model in my area, it's actually much quicker to set up. After I started my timer, I clocked in my installation process at about two minutes.&#160;</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B01HZD5MUM/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B01HZD5MUM&#38;linkId=6a37a6d9f9d7086e4495bcb220ac1691\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">ClearStream Eclipse Amplified</a> can mount to your wall by peeling tape on the back of the unit. You can take it down and put the model somewhere else, as well, and it will still hold up at a different location. It picks up a solid amount of channels thanks to its in-line amplifier, too. The small, external amplifier is simple to install, and the antenna itself is the most compact of all the units I tried.&#160;&#160;</p><p>Some of the channels I received include local CBS, Fox, NBC, and ABC. One downside is it doesn't pick up my local PBS channels or government channels, such as NYGov and NYLife, like some of the other models do.</p><p>This antenna also received the least amount of 1080i channels, six compared to the roughly 10 channels I received from other antennas. Still, I received zero choppy channels and had no trouble waiting for channels to appear on my screen. This stands out among the other models I tried.</p>\n\tThe best indoor antenna for easy setup\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064bee56183e10019819909?format=jpeg\" alt=\"mohu’s Leaf fifty antenna\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ben Blanchet/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1736471325802795306\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Mohu's Leaf Fifty</a> is an ultra-thin and easy to set up antenna with the same range as larger models.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>Design:</strong> Flat for wall or window</li><li><strong>Range:</strong> Up to 60 miles</li><li><strong>Amplifier:</strong> RF filtering low-noise antenna signal amplifier</li><li><strong>Channels received: </strong>74 during our testing</li></ul></aside><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Thin and subtle look, stable picture, wide range, easy setup, coaxial cable included</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Strong plastic smell after opening box</p><p>The <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1736471325802795306\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Mohu Leaf Fifty</a> is as thin as a sheet of paper but its range is strong compared to other, larger size models.</p><p>The <a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1736471325802795306\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Mohu Leaf</a> comes with a 16-foot coaxial cable and small push pins and tabs that you can use depending on how, and where, you want to place it. This enabled the easiest installation of any antenna I tested. The push pins are about the size of a single hair, and prevent the antenna from popping out on my wall like it would with tape behind it.</p><p>After I scanned for available channels, I picked up 74 stations including 10 channels with 1080i video and 11 channels in 720p. All of the major local channels were easily picked up, including Fox, CBS, NBC, and ABC. None of the channels were choppy and each loaded on my TV in a matter of seconds.</p><p>It should be noted, however, that just before I installed the antenna, there was a strong smell coming from the product. The odor went away after a few minutes but if you're sensitive to certain plastic scents, you may want to leave the box open a bit before installing right away.</p>\n\tHow we test antennas\n\t\n\t<p>All the antennas we test are either indoor-only antennas or models that are designed for both indoor and outdoor use. We tested each antenna at the same location under the same conditions at a third-floor apartment in the Astoria neighborhood of Queens, New York.&#160;</p><p>The same smart TV is used with each antenna. The units are set up about two feet from a window with no visible obstacles, like trees or wires outside of the building, that could impact the signal. All antennas are placed in the same location above or near the TV. We judge each antenna's channel support by comparing it to a list of channels that the <a href=\"http://www.antennaweb.org/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">AntennaWeb tool</a> predict will be available at our address.&#160;</p><p>We also account for cost and design when evaluating each model. We determine picture quality based on whether we notice any signal losses or choppiness during our testing period.</p><p>To test each antenna, we watch variety of channels for about 45 minutes. As far as the installation process goes, we use an iPhone timer to record the time it takes to unbox each antenna until it's set up near the TV.&#160;</p><p>One important takeaway from our testing is that the manufacturer's listed range does not necessarily translate to better performance compared to antennas with lower listed ranges. For instance, an antenna we tested with a listed range of 60 miles actually picks up fewer channels in our area than an antenna listed with a 35-mile range.&#160;</p><p>On that note, it's important to keep in mind that overall antenna performance will vary depending on your specific location.</p>\n\tWhat else we considered\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064bfa86183e1001981990e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Amazon Basics Amplified Indoor Outdoor TV antenna\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ben Blanchet/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>During our testing, we also considered a few other antennas. Here are the other antennas we evaluated for this guide, and why they didn't end up making the cut.&#160;&#160;</p><h3>Antennas we don't recommend:</h3><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07C3Y8SDH/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07C3Y8SDH&#38;linkId=8fa9ad196044b5dab1150e286b8a7a37\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Amazon Basics' Amplified Indoor/Outdoor TV antenna</a></strong>: While this model is around the median price of other units we looked at, it was the most complicated to set up. It took me roughly 20 minutes to install since the unit was missing a pair of screws in the package. Amazon did send me a replacement, however, which included the screws. This was also the largest model we tested, which makes it less convenient. And, while it got 70 channels on my first try, most of the 480p channels were choppy and broadcasts dropped in and out.&#160;</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B001GGAIIQ/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B001GGAIIQ&#38;linkId=1ba67330b5ad8ca82d35bea1d6096f59\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">RCA Multi-Directional Antenna</a></strong>: This antenna received the least amount channels &#8211; 42 &#8211; out of all the models I tried. Although the antenna is on the cheaper side compared to others, we recommend spending a bit more for a model with better reception.</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FClear-TV-Premium-HDTV-Antenna-As-Seen-on-TV%2F780888162\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Clear TV Premium HDTV Antenna</a></strong>: This is an antenna that might be familiar to infomercial watchers. The package comes with a salt shaker-size antenna and is one of the cheaper options I've come across. While the rabbit ear design could bring back memories, nine of its 68 channels &#8212; such as HSN, PBS, and Fox &#8212; appeared choppy on my TV. This is a decent option if you're looking for a bargain, but you can get better consistency with a slightly pricier model.</p>\n\tWhat we look forward to testing\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6064ce4cdaf0f10018f994e9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"antop antenna\" height=\"750\" width=\"1000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Other antennas we hope to try out in coming months include <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07XZ6RG34/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07XZ6RG34&#38;linkId=8a9f0ba3fc4b97d3c0f5c9f3be541074\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Antop's HD Smart Antenna SBS-301</a>. This model allows you to connect to two TVs at once and also claims to have a range of up to 80 miles.</p><p>There's also 1byOne's <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00IF70QCW/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B00IF70QCW&#38;linkId=4fd674f63e5ea164fe8219a096820569\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Indoor/Flat Amplified HDTV antenna</a>, a model that promises reception of channels up to 200 miles away. We also want to test Phillips' <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07D4YW5HR/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biip_020316_hdtv-antenna-buying-guide-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07D4YW5HR&#38;linkId=f8cc1c15ce74875d1f5c0e9d8f1f770f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Modern Loop Rabbit Ears Indoor TV antenna</a>. That model takes us back to our childhood with the classic, retro TV antenna design and also features a small size for easy placement.</p>\n\tAntenna FAQs\n\t\n\t<h3>What do I need before I purchase an antenna?</h3><p>Before you purchase an antenna, you'll want to make sure your TV includes an integrated digital tuner. This is standard for <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-tv-under-500-dollars\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">virtually any TV you can currently buy</a>, but if you still own a very old set you might need to purchase a separate digital tuner.</p><p>You'll also want to check whether or not the antenna you're considering comes with a coaxial cord. The cord is the only way you can connect your antenna to your TV so you'll need to buy a separate one if it's not included. If you want to place your antenna in the window or in a space away from your TV, you should measure the distance beforehand to see if the cord is long enough.</p><hr /><h3>What channels can I get with an antenna?</h3><p>Antennas pick up over-the-air broadcast channels that are available in your area. This typically means local networks like NBC, ABC, CBS, and Fox, along with a few dozen other stations. Channel availability, however, can drastically differ depending on whether your community is more rural or urban.&#160;</p><p>One way to check available channels in your community is through the <a href=\"http://www.antennaweb.org/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">AntennaWeb tool</a>. Just enter your address in the search bar and a list of channels that can be picked up in your area will show up in the results.</p><hr /><h3>Are there any limitations with an antenna?</h3><p>Antennas, unlike cable or streaming services, will only pick up local channels. If you want to see content from the likes of ESPN, AMC, FX, Disney Channel, and more, an antenna probably isn't for you. We recommend getting <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-much-is-sling-tv\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sling TV</a> ($35/month) for streaming access to more networks, as it's cheaper than most cable services.</p><p>Antenna reception can also be limited by external factors in your area. This means things like the amount of trees outside your home or nearby buildings could impact your viewing. The location of broadcast towers in your area, weather, and your room's shape and design can also impact your reception. In other words, the performance you get from an antenna can be rather finicky compared to cable and streaming.&#160;</p><p>Unlike most cable boxes, an antenna on its own won't let you record and store shows, though some external DVRs can be bought separately to record TV broadcasts from an antenna. Depending on your TV, you also might not get any kind of on-screen guide for navigation. This means, you have to manually go through each channel. With that said, some smart TVs now include guide integration for antenna playback.</p><hr /><h3>What video and audio quality can I get with an antenna?</h3><p>Most over-the-air broadcasts currently offer high definition (HD) picture quality with either 720p or 1080i resolution. This matches the resolution that most cable and live TV streaming services provide.&#160;</p><p>With that said, antenna-based broadcasts can actually look better than cable. Cable tends to compress video and audio quality more than antennas, so over-the-air TV will typically provide the clearest quality you can find in a broadcast. That is, as long as your reception is strong.</p><p>Over the next few years, some over-the-air stations will begin to broadcast in 4K through the new ATSC 3.0 standard, aka NextGenTV. NextGenTV's 4K broadcasts are already available in markets like Pittsburgh and Phoenix, and will make their way to cities like Buffalo and Orlando throughout 2021.&#160;</p><p>If you want to keep your current antenna, you can, but you'll have to buy an ATSC 3.0 tuner or a 4K TV with a built-in ATSC 3.0 tuner to actually watch in 4K. You can find more information on <a href=\"https://www.atsc.org/nextgen-tv/deployments/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">when 4K broadcasts will become available here</a>.</p><hr /><h3>Can I get local channels without an antenna?</h3><p>Yes. If you don't want to purchase an antenna or you don't already get local stations through cable, there are several streaming options that provide local channels over an internet connection.</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.locast.org/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Locast</a> streaming app offers local channels for free, but the service periodically interrupts streaming with donation requests unless you pay $5 a month to support the non-profit app. We don't recommend this as the best option, as it's cheaper to pay for an antenna in the long run, since the investment will pay off after a couple of months' use.</p><p>Other ways to stream local channels without an antenna include live TV streaming services like <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.sling.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Sling TV</a>, <a href=\"https://www.fubo.tv/welcome?irad=343747&#38;irmp=196318\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Fubo TV</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-watch-live-tv-on-hulu\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Hulu + Live TV</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-set-up-youtube-tv\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">YouTube TV</a>. Each service offers a different assortment of channels, including many cable networks you can't get with an antenna, so you'll want to ensure that the stations you want are available.</p>\n</div><div 02:15:08","updatedTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","title":"Poland is buying 5 cargo planes out of the US Air Force's 'boneyard'","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/poland-buying-cargo-planes-out-of-us-air-force-boneyard-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6076fb704206150018175676?format=jpeg\" alt=\"US Air Force C-130H\" height=\"700\" width=\"1400\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Airmen from the Wyoming Air National Guard prepare a C-130H for a mission out of Cheyenne, Wyoming, February 27, 2019.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Air Force/Master Sgt. Robert Trubia</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Poland is buying five C-130H Hercules aircraft out of the &#34;Boneyard&#34; in the Arizona desert.</li>\n<li>The aircraft will be partially retrofitted with new equipment, made flightworthy, and flown to Poland.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The Armament Inspectorate of the Polish Ministry of Defense published a release stating that an intergovernmental agreement has been signed on April 12, 2021, concerning the delivery of five <a href=\"https://theaviationist.com/2020/06/22/poland-to-acquire-c-130-airlifters-and-us-made-attack-helicopters-usaf-to-establish-presence-in-poland/\">C-130H airlifters to Poland</a>.</p><p>The deal is a part of the Excess Defense Articles grant program. The aircraft would be partially retrofitted with new equipment, made flightworthy, and then they would fly to Poland.</p><p>The agreement has a relatively low value - USD $14.3 million. The US side, the Polish MoD reports, assumes that five C-130H airframes that the <a href=\"https://theaviationist.com/2020/05/08/despite-the-covid-19-crisis-polish-air-force-f-16s-continue-intensive-flight-training-activities/\">Polish Air Force</a> would receive. They are worth $60 million, as per the US quote. The deliveries would be finalized by mid-2024, with the first aircraft arriving this year.</p><p>According to the Polish MoD, the aircraft procured rolled off the production line in 1985 and then were decommissioned in 2017. After that, they were stored at the <a href=\"https://theaviationist.com/2019/08/05/photo-captures-the-moment-as-lightning-strikes-a-c-5-galaxys-tail-at-the-amarg-boneyard-in-davis-monthan-afb/\">309th Aerospace Maintenance and Regeneration Group facility (AMARG)</a> in Tucson, Arizona. The above makes them 15 years younger than the C-130s currently operated by the Polish Air Force.</p><p>The technical status of the aircraft was assessed during the so-called Joint Visual Inspection procedure. It took place at AMARG in Tucson, stated the Inspectorate. The cost of the transfer to Poland was also a subject of this process.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5995baabb0e0b51c008b5b28?format=jpeg\" alt=\"C-130 Hercules takeoff landing gear\" height=\"2120\" width=\"3185\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>An Illinois Air National Guard C-130 Hercules takes off at Fort Carson in Colorado, September 12, 2016.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Air Force photo/Master Sgt. Joseph Swafford</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Then, after the transfer, the aircraft would undergo the periodic, scheduled maintenance (Programmed Depot Maintenance - PDM) at the WZL Nr 2 S.A. facility in Bydgoszcz, Poland. Bydgoszcz is also going to be the place where extra equipment, as required by the Polish Air Force, would be fitted onto the aircraft. Then the airframes are expected to become a part of the inventory of the 33rd Airlift Base in Powidz.</p><p>It has been pointed out by the experts that both the engines, as well as the propellers, along with the avionics, may need to be upgraded. What upgrades would be done within that scope remains unclear. However, to make the acquisition reasonable, the AMARG restoration work should also include an upgrade similar to the ones carried out in case of the ANG aircraft: a set of new T-56 Rolls Royce 3.5 engines and NP2000 eight-bladed propellers with electronic controls.</p><p>The PGZ Group&#39;s WZL facility in Bydgoszcz provides the Polish Air Force with a relevant maintenance capability regarding the Hercules.</p><p>The Polish MoD was putting the airlift capability enhancements in the modernization plans - the procurement was designated as the Drop program. It involved Leonardo S.p.A., Airbus Defence &#38; Space, Embraer, Lockheed Martin, and Boeing, but it was ultimately suspended in July last year. It seems that Poland went with second-hand airframes to serve as an intermediary gap-filler solution.</p><p>Krzysztof Płatek, spokesman for the Armament Inspectorate told us that the Drop program is to follow a schedule that is confidential. Procurement of the AMARG C-130s would diminish the pressure caused by deadlines and time.</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell.</a></strong></li>\n</ul><p>Coinbase is set to make its public trading debut on Wednesday and some market commentators are <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/coinbase-might-never-grow-into-its-valuation-1030300178\">questioning</a> its lofty valuation. Manhattan Venture Partners, an early backer of the crypto exchange, believes the massive figure is justified. </p><p>Santosh Rao, the head of research at the merchant bank, says a $100 billion valuation for Coinbase is &#34;totally reasonable&#34; given the disruptive nature of the crypto firm.</p><p>Manhattan Venture Partners was an early investor in Coinbase as well as a number of other big-name tech companies like SpaceX, Palantir, and Draft Kings.</p><p>Rao <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jQvh7QPEFSs\">sat down with CNBC</a> on Wednesday to discuss Coinbase&#39;s public debut and his firm&#39;s investments.</p><p>The head of research highlighted the fact that based on estimated revenues and earnings for 2022, at a roughly $100 billion valuation, Coinbase will trade at just over 11x sales and 27x EBITDA.</p><p>Those figures aren&#39;t outlandish for a company that has demonstrated consistent growth, according to Rao.</p><p>Coinbase released <a href=\"https://investor.coinbase.com/news/news-details/2021/Coinbase-Announces-First-Quarter-2021-Estimated-Results-and-Full-Year-2021-Outlook/default.aspx\">impressive first-quarter results</a> on April 6 that showed a 117% quarter-over-quarter increase in monthly transacting users. The company also <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/coinbase-earned-more-revenue-in-q1-than-all-of-2020-2021-4\">earned more revenue</a> in the first quarter of 2021 ($1.8 billion) than it did in all of 2020 ($1.3 billion).</p><p>The rising revenue came amid a historic run for <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/btc-usd\">bitcoin</a> that saw the cryptocurrency rise more than 300% in 2020, and an additional nearly 100% in the first quarter of 2021 alone.</p><p>Some market commentators are predicting a further <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-price-outlook-decisive-breakout-sets-up-for-further-gain-2021-4-1030299595\">10%+ breakout</a> moving forward as well.</p><p>When asked whether crypto prices need to keep going higher in order for Coinbase to maintain its lofty valuation, Rao said it would help, but argued the company has a range of services on offer to offset any downfall in crypto prices.</p><p>&#34;That&#39;s their core business at this point, but they have other services too. And they have a subscription product coming up, a whole range of services, the custody services, they have a number of other levers to pull as they go up,&#34; Rao said.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/bitcoin-contango-offers-risk-free-high-return-trade-opportunity-futures-2021-4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Bitcoin is a headache to store, and that&#39;s created an investment opportunity that could theoretically pay determined traders big risk-free returns by December</a></em></p><p>The head of research added that, in his view, there&#39;s no reason why crypto prices should stop going up as investors are starting to realize the space will become &#34;an integral part of the financial system going forward.&#34;</p><p>Rao also noted that of the best features of Coinbase is that it&#39;s &#34;agnostic&#34; towards individual cryptocurrencies, meaning if bitcoin falls and other cryptocurrencies rise, Coinbase will still benefit.</p><p>The head of research at Manhattan Venture Partners ended the interview by saying that Coinbase has the breadth, scale, and technology to keep competitors at bay over the long haul.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a (Will Daniel)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/6076f1ac4206150018175624?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn17@2020_5/2021/04/14/18-15-35-145_fb01185b799ad817.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn1@2020_2/2021/04/14/18-15-35-145_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=mYy_VSCGd_Y:7wUAXVGBbes:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn19@2020_1/2021/04/14/18-15-28-973_9d393bdf91ee119f.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=mYy_VSCGd_Y:7wUAXVGBbes:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn65@2020_2/2021/04/14/18-15-29-769_1930571345bca80a.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn29@2020_4/2021/04/14/18-15-29-996_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=mYy_VSCGd_Y:7wUAXVGBbes:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn9@2020_6/2021/04/14/18-15-36-221_ba4f557a74dc5092.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/mYy_VSCGd_Y":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn61@2020_2/2021/04/14/18-15-30-586_7c3127dad5d0c16c.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1618424108841},{"createdTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","updatedTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","title":"Billionaire Jack Ma was one of China's biggest success stories. The government turning on him speaks to an animosity against billionaires in the Communist country.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/why-china-cracked-down-jack-ma-ant-group-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fa420631df1d500182190d1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Jack Ma\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2222\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Wang HE/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>China has cracked down on Jack Ma and his companies Ant Group and Alibaba recently.</li>\n<li>The government may be targeting him, but China is also focused on reining in billionaires at large.</li>\n<li>A wealth gap has widened, posing issues for the communist nation, which strives for distributed wealth.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>When Jack Ma&#39;s <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/ant-group-ipo-suspended-shanghai-hong-kong-china-regulators-2020-11-1029758861\">Ant Group IPO was yanked by Chinese regulators</a> last fall, it was easy to view it as merely a sign of China&#39;s firm hand.</p><p>Ant had ballooned into an independent force alongside the state-controlled Chinese bank system, and the halted listing came just after Ma brazenly and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-happened-ant-group-ipo-jack-ma-alipay-2020-11\">publicly criticized the nation&#39;s banking rules</a>. Simply put, he spoke out against the country&#39;s lack of a traditional financial system and the large role that the Party plays in lending money, as <a href=\"https://asia.nikkei.com/Spotlight/Most-read-in-2020/Jack-Ma-vs.-the-Party-Inside-the-collapse-of-the-world-s-biggest-IPO\">Nikkei Asia</a> reported.</p><p>News later surfaced that <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/ant-group-ipo-personally-halted-china-xi-jinping-jack-wsj-2020-11-1029800224\">Chinese President Xi Jinping personally instructed authorities</a> to look into Ant. Now, Ant - <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-happened-ant-group-ipo-jack-ma-alipay-2020-11\">which was once praised as a fintech disruptor</a> on the global stage - will likely, eventually, be majorly run by the state.</p><p>But the government&#39;s takedown of Ma may be indicative of a larger zeroing-in on billionaires in the country as an existing wealth gap grows wider, a gap that has been exacerbated by the pandemic. </p><p>Disdain for the Communist country&#39;s affluent population has grown, as the <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2020/12/24/technology/china-jack-ma-alibaba.html\">New York Times</a> reported, and the government is leaning into that anti-rich sentiment as it&#39;s broken down the power constructs that Ma has built in the country.</p><h2>A widening wealth gap in China</h2><p>Communist China once embraced a more capitalist-friendly free market in the 1980s, and when it did, some citizens saw their wealth skyrocket, as <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/features/2020-12-09/china-rich-kids-try-to-avoid-being-target-as-xi-tackles-wealth-gap\">Bloomberg</a> reported in December. Solidified social classes emerged, making it easier for the wealthy to maintain and grow their fortunes - but also more difficult for lower-income people to get richer.</p><p>Today&#39;s rising housing costs in China&#39;s cities and a squeezed white-collar job market with lower pay presents problems for the country&#39;s young and educated in securing financial stability, per the NYT report. Those woes have stirred an animosity of the wealthy in China - as Bloomberg reported, the children who were born into money now find themselves under the scornful eye of the nation&#39;s leader.</p><p>Besides the US, China has the most billionaires out of every country in the world - 626 to be exact, according to <a href=\"https://www.forbes.com/sites/jenniferwang/2021/04/06/the-10-richest-chinese-billionaires-in-2021/?sh=30924ded5ca2\">Forbes.</a> Beijing itself has more billionaires than any city in the world. But about 600 million of its <a href=\"https://www.statista.com/statistics/263765/total-population-of-china/\">1.4 billion</a>-strong population earn $150 a month or less, as the <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2020/12/24/technology/china-jack-ma-alibaba.html\">NYT</a> notes.</p><p>Such economic disparities have caused political problems for the Chinese Communist Party, which strives to preserve an evenly distributed wealth system. And Ma, with his <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/inspiring-life-story-of-alibaba-founder-jack-ma-2017-2#:~:text=He's%20currently%20worth%20about%20%2450%20billion.ion.\">$50 billion in net worth</a>, is among its targets.</p><p>With a widening wealth gap, and billionaires like Jack Ma exhibiting that their companies can grow into the powerhouses that they are, China is hell-bent on preventing <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/china-economy-politburo/china-to-keep-economic-operations-within-reasonable-range-in-2021-politburo-idINKBN28L1H0\">&#34;the disorderly expansion of capital,&#34;</a> as Chinese leadership said in December.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6077106974da0300181e1a24?format=jpeg\" alt=\"alibaba jack ma NYSE\" height=\"1113\" width=\"1485\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Alibaba went public on the NYSE in 2014.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Andrew Burton/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>China is tightening its grip on its economy</h2><p>China is singling out companies and figures across industries in its quest to rein in the economy, from <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/hm-boycott-wiped-from-internet-china-2021-3\">Swedish retailer H&#38;M</a> to homegrown tech giants, which have largely enjoyed a lack of regulatory constraints.</p><p>The government <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/alibaba-ceo-daniel-zhang-china-rules-timely-necessary-2020-11\">rolled out a set of new anti-competitive behavior rules</a> for internet companies like Alibaba in November. It included guidelines to prevent companies from sharing sensitive user data and from joining together to stomp out smaller competitors.</p><p>Alibaba CEO <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/alibaba-ceo-daniel-zhang-china-rules-timely-necessary-2020-11\">Daniel Zhang said shortly after that he welcomed the new rules.</a> And last week, Chinese authorities fined <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/jack-ma-alibaba-group-28-billion-antitrust-fine-china-2021-4\">Alibaba what equals $2.8 billion USD</a> over concerns that it was abusing its dominant market position.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/alibaba-antitrust-cloud-amazon-microsoft-google-big-tech-analyst-2020-12?r=kc-sub\">China&#39;s antitrust probe into Alibaba could be an opportunity for other cloud players - including Amazon, Microsoft, and Google - to swoop in</a></em></p><p>China was hoping other tech giants would take it as a warning, and it looks like they have. About three dozen Chinese tech companies, including TikTok owner Bytedance, JD.com, and the Twitter-like Weibo, have vowed to adhere to China&#39;s new anti-competitive laws, according to a report from the <a href=\"https://www.wsj.com/articles/chinas-tech-giants-vow-in-unison-to-play-by-regulators-rules-11618402448\">Wall Street Journal.</a> They are also pledging to keep the party&#39;s values at the forefront of their minds in hopes of escaping Ma&#39;s fate.</p><p>The Ma-China debacle signals that turbulent times may lie ahead for innovation in China, as the Communist Party and its leaders demand that the country&#39;s business community put patriotism above all else. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Shelley Moore Capito of West Virginia said a middle ground between Democrats and Republicans on an infrastructure deal would be significantly less than half of the $2.3 trillion package that President Joe Biden seeks.</p><p>&#34;I think the best way for us to do this is hit the sweet spot of where we agree and I think we can agree on a lot of the measures moving forward. How much? I would say probably into the $600 or $800 billion, but we haven&#39;t put all of that together yet,&#34; Capito <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2iv0lo7M0VM\">told CNBC.</a></p><p>Capito laid out some potential revenue elements, including unused coronavirus relief funds, road usage fees for electric cars, and a vehicle miles-traveled tax. She also suggested raising the gas tax, a measure the Biden administration <a href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/2021/04/13/gas-tax-not-considered-in-biden-infrastructure-plan-white-house-says.html\">has already ruled out.</a></p><p>&#34;It&#39;s going to have to come from a lot of different sources, but this is important,&#34; she said. Capito did not bring up lifting corporate taxes.</p><p>The West Virginia Republican later told Capitol Hill reporters there was a group were drafting a counterproposal, suggesting it would be sized somewhere between $600 billion to $800 billion. Capito was part of the Republican group that pitched a $618 billion counterproposal, which Biden along with Democrats ultimately rejected.</p><p>Other Republicans are signaling they are putting together a new package. Sen. Mitt Romney of Utah told reporters on Capitol Hill Wednesday there is a bipartisan group of 20 lawmakers evenly divided between Republicans and Democrats drafting one.</p><p>Then Sen. Bill Cassidy of Louisiana <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/gop-infrastructure-plan-double-biden-spending-roads-bridges-cassidy-2021-4\">said on Tuesday</a> that a bipartisan group was assembling an &#34;alternative&#34; to the Biden plan. He indicated it would double the amount of spending on roads and bridges from the $115 billion that the president is seeking.</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-in-bidens-infrastructure-bill-package-american-jobs-plan-2021-3\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"d37f5a88eac00946ba399e198e403bcc\">Biden infrastructure plan</a> includes major funding to fix roads and bridges and set up clean energy incentives. It also has federal funds for in-home elder care, public transit, and schools, among other areas.</p><p>Democrats are pressing to take advantage of the cheap cost of borrowing to fund new investments they say will curb inequality and grow the economy.</p><p>Republicans, however, are opposed to the Biden package, viewing it as a colossal liberal wish-list. Capito criticized the Biden proposal&#39;s expansive scope, arguing it should be constrained to roads, bridges, airports, broadband, and water infrastructure.</p><p>&#34;If we&#39;re going to do this together, which we want to do and is our desire, we&#39;ve got to find those areas and take away the extra infrastructure areas that the president put into his bill like home health aides and school building and all of these kinds of things,&#34; she told CNBC.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 02:15:08","updatedTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","title":"The CDC says airplanes should leave middle seats empty to reduce COVID-19 spread - after every major US airline decided it was unnecessary","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-leaving-middle-seat-empty-on-airplanes-reduces-covid-spread-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e96ccec29d6d9477b2efd43?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Kanye Airplane\" height=\"1315\" width=\"2879\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Not a great idea anymore.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vgLOv36an3s\" target=\"_blank\">&#34;The Late Late Show with James Corden&#34;</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>A CDC study estimated that keeping middle seats empty may <strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\">reduce &#34;viable virus&#34; exposure by up to 57%.</strong></li>\n<li><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\">In the modeling study, the mannequins didn&#39;t wear any masks.</strong></li>\n<li><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\">It&#39;s a reminder that masks plus distance is best, especially if passengers remove their masks.</strong></li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>This summer, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/delta-airlines-to-stop-blocking-middle-seats-in-may-2021-3\">every major US airline</a> will have middle seats open to purchase on planes.</p><p>But a new Centers for Disease Control and Prevention study suggests that could be a great way to invite COVID-19 to spread aboard flights, especially when passengers might lower their masks to eat or drink.</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/mmwr/volumes/70/wr/mm7016e1.htm?s_cid=mm7016e1_w\">CDC report</a>, out Wednesday, estimated how far coronavirus aerosols (airborne particles that can linger) could spread on a plane. To do this, researchers modeled how a similar virus spread among mannequins in a lab when they weren&#39;t wearing masks.</p><p>The study found that leaving middle seats empty to space out passengers and their germs could help reduce viral exposure in flight when people take off their masks or if their masks have gaps in them.</p><p>For instance, the study found that sitting two seats from an infectious person could reduce a passenger&#39;s risk of exposure to &#34;viable virus&#34; particles by 23% compared with their risk sitting right next to an infectious person with their mask off. That risk could be reduced by as much as 57% in a three-row section with vacant middle seats.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6076ff4b74da0300181e197e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"cdc plane study covid transmission \" height=\"406\" width=\"716\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/mmwr/volumes/70/wr/mm7016e1.htm?s_cid=mm7016e1_w\" target=\"_blank\">CDC MMWR</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>While masks are now required apparel on major airlines and very few cases of COVID-19 spreading aboard planes have been documented during the pandemic, masks aren&#39;t perfect at trapping viral aerosols in flight.</p><p>A <a href=\"https://wwwnc.cdc.gov/eid/article/27/5/21-0514_article\">recent case study</a> from New Zealand suggested that even masked airline passengers who have COVID-19 could emit aerosols capable of infecting passengers around them.</p><p>The new CDC study, though an imperfect approximation of how people behave on planes during the pandemic, is a good reminder that layers of protection - masks, distance, <em>and</em> frequent handwashing - are much better at preventing the spread of the virus than a single protocol.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-leaving-middle-seat-empty-on-airplanes-reduces-covid-spread-2021-4'>Business time - and knocking down the $80 million Palm Beach mansion he just bought. </p><p>The Oracle billionaire sent an email to employees this week explaining his future plans after <a href=\"https://www.wsj.com/articles/hedge-funder-sells-palm-beach-mansion-for-80-million-11617917824\">reports surfaced</a> that he had purchased a 15,000-square-foot home in South Florida. Ellison confirmed that he had purchased the mansion, but that he&#39;s &#34;tearing the house down and not moving to Florida,&#34; according to <a href=\"https://www.vox.com/recode/2021/4/12/22380192/larry-ellison-lanai-hawaii-palm-beach-mansion\">Recode&#39;s Theodore Schleifer</a>.</p><p>&#34;Last year I moved from California to the island of Lana&#39;i and became a resident of the State of Hawaii,&#34; Ellison wrote. &#34;I love it here and have no plans to move back to Florida, Texas, back to California ... or anywhere else.&#34;</p><p>Ellison&#39;s <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/larry-ellison-oracle-palm-beach-mansion-photos-2021-4\"> home in Palm Beach</a> sits on 7.35 acres, making it the third-largest oceanfront parcel of land in Palm Beach County, according to a real estate listing. The Tuscan-style home, which previously belonged to hedge-fund manager Gabe Hoffman, includes seven bedrooms, 11 bathrooms and three half-bathrooms, a VIP guest suite, a home theater, a wine room, a chef&#39;s kitchen, a swimming pool, and a tennis court.</p><p>The home was built in 1998, and it&#39;s unclear why Ellison would want to knock it down. Ellison already has an <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/larry-ellison-real-estate-2015-4\">extensive real estate portfolio</a> that includes multimillion-dollar homes in San Francisco, Malibu, Lake Tahoe, Rhode Island, and Japan.</p><p><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/palm-beach-florida-the-season-pandemic-parties-restaurants-masks-2021-2\" data-e2e-name=\"inline-read-more-link\">Peek into Palm Beach&#39;s wild, sometimes maskless pandemic party scene as wealthy residents carry on &#39;living their lives&#39;</a></em></p><p>But it seems the tech mogul, who&#39;s <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/billionaires/profiles/lawrence-j-ellison/\">worth $91.5 billion</a>, has no plans to live in the mansion, or anywhere else in the contiguous United States. </p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/larry-ellison-oracle-lanai-island-hawaii-move-2020-12\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\" data-uri=\"66e544f13c39e908db0c17fff83636cc\">Ellison revealed last year</a> that he had moved to Lanai, Hawaii, amid the coronavirus pandemic. He plans to use &#34;the power of Zoom to work&#34; from the island, he wrote in an email to Oracle employees at the time, who had been asking about Ellison&#39;s plans in the wake of Oracle <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/oracle-moving-to-austin-hq-silicon-valley-texas-2020-12\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\" data-uri=\"61456b67e228ef28b789ca50c528edb6\">moving its headquarters to Austin, Texas</a>. </p><p>Ellison purchased nearly 98% of the island of Lanai in 2012 for a reported $300 million - his purchase included 87,000 of the island&#39;s 90,000 acres of land. Lanai, which is home to about 3,200 residents, is the smallest inhabited island in Hawaii and is home to serene beaches, rugged terrain, high-end resorts, as well as <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/oracle-larry-ellison-lanai-hawaii-plans-sustainability-tourism-2020-12\">Ellison&#39;s sustainability ambitions</a>, which he&#39;s executing through a development company called Pulama Lanai. </p><p>He also launched a wellness company called Sensei in 2018, which is working on three main issues: global food supply, nutrition, and sustainability. Sensei has since launched two 20,000-square-foot hydroponic greenhouses on the island, known as Sensei Farms, and a luxury spa called Sensei Retreat that costs $3,000 a night. </p><div 02:15:08","updatedTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","title":"Senate Republicans to discuss repealing ban on earmarks, key tactic for passing difficult legislation","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/earmarks-senate-republicans-ban-bring-back-community-funding-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/601c299bee136f00183aa511?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Mitt Romney\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2222\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Sen. Mitt Romney (R-UT).\n<p class=\"copyright\">Caroline Brehman/CQ-Roll Call, Inc via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The Senate GOP will meet next week to decide on bringing earmarks, funding members can use for their districts, back.</li>\n<li>This follows House Republicans approving the restoration of earmarks in March.</li>\n<li>Some GOP Senators opposed bringing earmarks back because of past abuses with the funding measure.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Almost a month after House Republicans <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/earmarks-house-republicans-vote-to-approve-repeal-ban-congress-2021-3\">voted</a> to approve the restoration of earmarks, Senate Republicans are expected to meet next week to discuss bringing back the so-called community funding measures.</p><p>A decade ago, Republicans banned earmarks, which allow members to put funding for their districts in a larger bill, following a series of scandals related to earmark abuses. But now, both House Democrats and House Republicans have voted to bring them back, and Senate Republicans are set to meet next Wednesday to ratify their rules and discuss earmark usage, <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2021-04-13/senate-gop-nearing-decision-on-whether-to-embrace-earmarks\">according</a> to Bloomberg.</p><p>As some moderate Democrats, notably Sen. Joe Manchin of West Virginia, stress the importance of bipartisan legislation, earmarks could be an important tactic for easing difficult legislation through congress on bipartisan lines.</p><p>Republican Sen. Richard Shelby of Alabama <a href=\"https://thehill.com/homenews/senate/547837-senate-gop-opens-door-to-earmarks\">told</a> The Hill on Tuesday that Democrats are already going forward with restoring earmarks, so he thinks &#34;the decision is headed toward letting every member decide if they want to participate in the earmark process.&#34;</p><p>On March 2, House Democrats <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/house-committee-introduces-new-community-project-funding-guidelines-2021-3\">introduced</a> new guidelines for earmarks to bring them back while increasing transparency and requiring members to verify they have no financial interest in the funding requests, among other things.</p><p>On March 17, House Republicans <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/earmarks-house-republicans-vote-to-approve-repeal-ban-congress-2021-3\">voted by secret ballot</a> to bring earmarks back as well. House Minority Leader Kevin McCarthy said after the vote that there was &#34;real concern&#34; about solely the Biden administration directing where money goes.</p><p>&#34;This doesn&#39;t add one more dollar,&#34; McCarthy said. &#34;I think members here know what&#39;s most important about what&#39;s going on in their district, not Biden.&#34;</p><p>However, some Senate Republicans did not feel the same. Sen. Mitt Romney of Utah told reporters after the vote that earmarks &#34;are not the right way to go.&#34;</p><p>&#34;They have been associated with excess, and it would represent a turn to the worst,&#34; he said.</p><p>The ban on earmarks once had <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/earmarks-reinstatement-democrats-republicans-ban-2021-3\">bipartisan support</a>, as a series of scandals led to former President Barack Obama saying in 2011 that he would veto any bill containing earmarks. </p><p>A defining earmark scandal occurred in 2005, when Alaska Rep. Don Young secured $233 million for a bridge that would connect two small cities, which became known as the &#34;<a href=\"https://thehill.com/homenews/house/268303-gop-lawmaker-drops-exception-to-earmark-ban\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"ca965871f5c78f3d7eb1ae79d14fe9c8\">bridge to nowhere</a>,&#34; as critics said the bridge would not significantly benefit Young&#39;s community. The same year, former California Rep. Duke Cunningham landed himself eight years in prison for accepting <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trumps-pardon-largesse-a-boon-for-well-connected-fraudsters-2021-1\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"bc3c4263c5211854d4b9ba678f26f2d4\">$2.4 million in bribes</a> in return for promising earmarks to defense contractors.</p><p>As recently as March 1, a group of 10 Republican senators, led by Sens. Marco Rubio of Florida and Steve Daines of Montana, introduced a bill to permanently ban earmarks. Rubio said in a <a href=\"https://www.rubio.senate.gov/public/index.cfm?p=Press-Releases&id=4FDA53F0-546A-4E05-869E-7D4C24753E4F3E4F\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"718e2390a28896dec1fd66e59db02989\">statement</a> that earmarks had led to &#34;corruption and waste, and bought votes in Congress for unpopular legislation.&#34;</p><p>Although Republican lawmakers have <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/kristi-noem-infrastructure-pipes-south-dakota-governor-republicans-fox-news-2021-4\">largely opposed</a> President Joe Biden&#39;s infrastructure plan thus far, bringing earmarks back could help pass difficult legislation as it allows lawmakers to include funding for their specific districts in bills.</p><p>The House is already using earmarks again, and the Transportation and Infrastructure Committee is accepting member requests for community funding through April 23 .</p><div 02:15:08","updatedTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","title":"Senate Democrats want to replace most of your lost paycheck with permanently boosted unemployment benefits","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/senate-democrats-unemployment-benefits-congress-wyden-bennet-benefits-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6076f374420615001817562e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Ron Wyden\" height=\"1000\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Sen. Ron Wyden (D-OR).\n<p class=\"copyright\">Photo by Win McNamee/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Senate Democrats have unveiled a plan to boost unemployment benefits permanently.</li>\n<li>The plan aims to replace 75% of a worker&#39;s lost paycheck.</li>\n<li>It also sets up a $250 weekly benefit for gig workers who don&#39;t qualify for regular unemployment.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>A pair of Senate Democrats introduced a plan on Wednesday to permanently boost unemployment benefits, making state checks larger to cover most of a worker&#39;s lost wages.</p><p>The plan from Sens. Ron Wyden of Oregon and Michael Bennet of Colorado would mandate states to replace up to 75% of a person&#39;s income at their last job. It also sets up a $250 &#34;jobseeker allowance&#34; for gig workers and contractors - essentially a weekly benefit that replaces Pandemic Unemployment Assistance so those types of workers are no longer barred from receiving state unemployment.</p><p>Gig workers have secured access to unemployment benefits in 2020 and 2021, but only on an emergency basis via the pandemic-related stimulus programs. Currently, laid-off workers are eligible under PUA for <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stimulus-senate-democrats-broker-deal-on-unemployment-benefits-2021-3\">a $300 weekly federal unemployment benefit</a> - on top of state payouts - which is slated to end on Labor Day.</p><p>&#34;Unemployment programs are critical to helping workers stay afloat during difficult times - but too many workers still struggle to access their benefits in our patchwork of outdated state systems,&#34; Wyden said in a statement.</p><p>&#34;This proposal will protect workers by strengthening and expanding benefits, modernize UI infrastructure with needed technology investments, and prepare us for the future by tying benefits to economic conditions&#34; Bennet said.</p><p>The plan also requires states to provide a minimum 26 weeks of unemployment benefits, <a href=\"https://www.cbpp.org/research/economy/how-many-weeks-of-unemployment-compensation-are-available\">which varies greatly</a> from one state to another. An additional 13 weeks are triggered if the unemployment rate climbs above 6.5% at the national or state level, tying the flow of aid to economic conditions.  More weeks would become available if the jobless rate surges.</p><p>Under the proposal, states face some tax penalties if they break from these standards. It&#39;s unclear whether the unemployment reforms will eventually form part of Biden&#39;s infrastructure package.</p><p>Last year, state unemployment offices were overwhelmed with a surge of claims that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-states-unemployment-insurance-programs-ended-in-disaster-2020-9\">strained their antiquated systems</a> to the brink. They struggled to implement a $600 benefit, keeping people from accessing critical aid as the economy tanked due to the pandemic. Democrats and labor advocates are seeking to modernize them to prevent similar chaos.</p><p>Most Republicans opposed the renewal of boosted federal unemployment benefits as the economy showed signs of recovering. They argued the federal assistance discouraged people from returning to work.</p><p>Republican lawmakers in three states are advancing plans to cut the number of weeks unemployed people can get benefits, <a href=\"https://www.huffpost.com/entry/unemployment-insurance-republican-cuts_n_60749ea8e4b0cd39fcc0465a\">HuffPost reported.</a></p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article Here are the 18 best quotes.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/shark-tank-kevin-oleary-gamestop-spacs-warns-stock-market-crash-2021-4","description":"<p><strong><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5429cf3becad04741a31ea09?format=jpeg\" alt=\"kevin o&#39;leary\" height=\"615\" width=\"1231\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Kevin O&#39;Leary.\n<p class=\"copyright\">REUTERS/ Gus Ruelas</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></strong></p><ul><li><strong>Kevin O&#39;Leary touted GameStop, Robinhood, and NFTs in an interview this week.</strong></li><li><strong>The &#34;Shark Tank&#34; investor warned about airlines, leverage, and celebrity SPACs.</strong></li><li><strong>O&#39;Leary also blasted prospective tax hikes and took aim at China.</strong></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</strong></li></ul><p>&#34;Shark Tank&#34; investor Kevin O&#39;Leary suggested GameStop could <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/gamestop-stock-netflix-comeback-shark-tank-kevin-oleary-short-sellers-2021-4-1030302964\">execute a Netflix-style comeback</a>, predicted several US airlines will go bankrupt over the next two years, and warned of a brutal market correction in an <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FBuXIBeepC0&t=34m20sm20sm20s\">interview this week</a>.</p><p>The O&#39;Leary Funds and O&#39;Leary Ventures boss  - whose nickname is Mr. Wonderful - also slammed celebrity SPACs, praised Robinhood, and trumpeted NFTs during the conversation with influencer Kevin Paffrath on his YouTube channel, Meet Kevin.</p><p>O&#39;Leary also criticized the Biden administration&#39;s plan to hike corporate taxes, and called for the US to take a tougher stance towards China.</p><h2>Here are O&#39;Leary&#39;s best quotes from the interview, lightly edited and condensed for clarity:</h2><p>1. &#34;I&#39;m waiting. So far there&#39;s been no correction, but I&#39;ve lived through lots of volatility and I know, just when it seems to be safe, poo poo happens.&#34; - <em>discussing the prospect of a market crash.</em></p><p>2. &#34;GameStop&#39;s brand has way more value today than it had five months ago, before it became part of every headline around the world, day after day. Netflix saw the writing on the wall when they were mailing DVDs to everybody and said, &#39;We&#39;re going to digitize this,&#39; and they had a brand. Maybe GameStop can do the same thing.&#34;</p><p>3. &#34;If I was short GameStop stock right now, I&#39;d be worried. I think it&#39;s going to get a second kick at life. This whole social constituency supporting it - the pricing of the stock is kind of irrelevant at this point.&#34;</p><p>4. &#34;It&#39;s hilarious if you look at the volatility of Amazon over the last 20 years. You would have never owned it as it&#39;s so volatile, but in the long run it&#39;s created a trillion dollars&#39; worth of value for shareholders. Same thing is going to happen to these stocks that are going to provide digitization.&#34; - <em>underscoring the growth prospects of Zoom, Shopify, and other stocks that enable remote activities.</em></p><p>5. &#34;It&#39;s not good news for the airlines because even though they&#39;re coming back, it&#39;s all basically vacation tickets. Everybody&#39;s going to Disneyland in a big tube. That&#39;s a very crappy business, they won&#39;t make any money. Over the next two years, probably a couple of them have to go bankrupt.&#34; - <em>underscoring the challenges for airlines if business travel permanently falls by 15% or 20%.</em></p><p>6. &#34;Frankly I&#39;m not a big fan of SPACs. I do have about 20 SPACs in my portfolio right now, but only from operators that I know. A SPAC is no different than private equity, and so I need to know the team that&#39;s backing the SPAC has done deals before, knows how to buy at the right multiple, and knows how to operate. I&#39;m against the idea that some celebrity knows what they&#39;re doing in private equity, it&#39;s a joke. I avoid those like the plague, I think those are going to go to zero.&#34;</p><p>7. &#34;I&#39;m a big fan of Robinhood because even though it&#39;s got a lot of criticism, it helps 22 million people learn about stocks. I&#39;m a big believer in learning the ways of the stock market.&#34;</p><p>8. &#34;When you get into these complex straddles and collars and all of this stuff with leverage, sometimes you wake up with a hangover after going out to a party, and you forget the position you have on and you just blow yourself up. You&#39;ve got to be careful.&#34;</p><p>9. &#34;I&#39;m beyond sanctions, I want to take them right out of the financial system in North America.&#34; - <em>calling for the US to adopt a tougher stance towards China in order to level the playing field.</em></p><p>10. &#34;Elon Musk is a maverick who doesn&#39;t play by the rules, but he&#39;s actually a good example of how this relationship should work. If American companies want to go to China, they shouldn&#39;t have to give up control of their intellectual property to do that.&#34;<em><br></em></p><p>11. &#34;If you believe that burning up huge amounts of coal is detrimental and I do, you should stop buying bitcoin from the Chinese. Over time, as institutions start to really get involved in crypto, you&#39;ll have the discounted blood coin from China and you&#39;ll have the premium virgin coin with provenance - no different than blood diamonds.&#34;</p><p>12. &#34;NFTs are a derivative of the digital economy. There&#39;s merit, but as a new asset class it&#39;s going to be immensely volatile. The idea that you have something that&#39;s copyrighted in perpetuity and can&#39;t be forged is really interesting and a good idea. At the end of the day they will find their place.&#34;</p><p>13. &#34;You&#39;re pouring free money out of the sky from a helicopter into anywhere you can stuff it. But then you&#39;re raising taxes so you&#39;re taking it back right away, before it has a chance to have any effect whatsoever. You can&#39;t suck and blow at the same time, it doesn&#39;t make any sense.&#34; - <em>criticizing the Biden administration&#39;s plan to follow up its stimulus efforts by raising corporate taxes.</em></p><p>14. &#34;The idea that Yellen can <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/janet-yellen-corporate-tax-global-minimum-overhaul-oecd-treasury-2021-3\">run around the world</a> asking for a standard minimum corporate tax is a joke that&#39;s never going to happen.&#34;</p><p>15. &#34;I covet downside protection much more than outperformance. I don&#39;t care about beating the indexes at all. I don&#39;t need more money, I need to keep what I&#39;ve got.&#34;</p><p>16. &#34;Buying the dip is more rock and roll, but what invariably happens is you go through a massive correction and you learn a very important lesson. The generation that is trading right now has never gone through a sustained correction. It&#39;s coming - I don&#39;t know when, I don&#39;t know what&#39;ll trigger it, but they will learn their lesson. If you have a lot of leverage on, it&#39;s a hell of a lesson because you end up in a negative net-worth position. But you do learn from it.&#34;</p><p>17. &#34;Take 10% of your paycheck, put it away, and do not touch it except in emergencies. When you take money and burn it on a vacation, or buy some useless piece of crap you&#39;re never going to use - which many people are guilty of including me - you&#39;ve killed off your future. That money&#39;s not working for you anymore. Do you really need another pair of jeans, another pair of shoes? Just look at your closet of all the crap you don&#39;t wear, that&#39;s all money you wasted.&#34;</p><p>18. &#34;If you walk around with an Apple Watch on, that thing is a piece of consumer-electronic junk. I own Apple stock, but I would never be seen dead with an Apple Watch. Not a chance in hell.&#34; - <em>voicing his preference for wearing traditional watches and supporting conventional watchmakers.</em></p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a
