Waiters and waitresses make an annual salary of $22,940.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d519f4fd0c4360208486600?format=jpeg\" alt=\"restaurant waiter\" height=\"3840\" width=\"5120\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Associated Press</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 2,110</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/35-3031.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>: Waiters and waitresses take orders from customers and serve food and drinks at restaurants or cafes.</p>\n\t16. Lifeguards, ski patrol, and other recreational protective service workers make an annual salary of $23,550.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/563cb3c0bd86ef16008c7df9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"lifeguard\" height=\"1960\" width=\"2613\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A lifeguard runs into the water to rescue a youth that was calling for help in heavy surf due to being caught in a rip current on the Windward side of Oahu, Hawaii.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"http://pictures.reuters.com/C.aspx?VP3=SearchResult&#38;VBID=2C0BXZJQ697JG&#38;SMLS=1&#38;RW=1344&#38;RH=850#/SearchResult&#38;VBID=2C0BXZJQ697JG&#38;SMLS=1&#38;RW=1344&#38;RH=850&#38;PN=2&#38;POPUPPN=111&#38;POPUPIID=2C0408WUUZ4EI\" target=\"_blank\">Reuters/Carlo Allegri</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong>&#160;5,330</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/33-9092.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>:&#160;Lifeguards, ski patrol, and other recreational protective service workers make sure people are safe in amusement parks, whether they're in the pool or on the slopes.</p>\n\t15. Fast food and counter attendants make an annual salary of $24,060.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d44935d100a2437bd15c1a7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"cafeteria\" height=\"1369\" width=\"1825\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">zoranm/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 11,980</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/35-3022.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>:&#160;Counter attendants serve food to customers from counters or steam tables. This job category includes cafe servers, cafeteria workers, and snack bar attendants.</p>\n\t14. Amusement and recreation attendants make an annual salary of $24,310.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6077031e42061500181756b1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Universal Studios in Orlando, Florida\" height=\"1285\" width=\"1714\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visitors attend the Universal Studios theme park first day of reopening from the coronavirus pandemic, on June 05, 2020 in Orlando, Florida.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Gerardo Mora/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 28,640</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/39-3091.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>: Amusement and recreation attendants operate amusement concessions, kiosks, or rides, and maintain amusement park supplies and equipment.</p>\n\t13. Recreation workers make an annual salary of $24,320.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d8a2c48f4fc24473b738232?format=jpeg\" alt=\"amusement theme park worker\" height=\"1350\" width=\"1800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dale Sparks/AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 1,410</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/39-9032.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong><a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/39-9032.00\"></a>: Recreation workers organize and promote activities, including arts and crafts, sports, games, music, and other social activities.</p>\n\t12. Maids and housekeeping cleaners make an annual salary of $24,340.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607705e974da0300181e19b9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"housekeeping\" height=\"1295\" width=\"1726\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">andresr/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades: </strong>2,580</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/37-2012.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Maids and housekeeping cleaners' duties may include cleaning rooms, making beds, and vacuuming.</p>\n\t11. Cashiers make an annual salary of $25,110.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6077065374da0300181e19c1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Walt Disney World Resort\" height=\"1300\" width=\"1733\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Kent Phillips/Walt Disney World Resort/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 4,990</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/41-2011.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>:&#160;Cashiers handle customers' money using cash registers or scanners.&#160;</p>\n\t10. Janitors and cleaners make an annual salary of $25,350.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d531f74cd978420c13b529b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"janitor\" height=\"957\" width=\"1276\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Matilde Campodonico/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 3,620</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/37-2011.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>: Janitors and cleaners keep buildings clean and orderly using equipment ranging from brooms and mops to carpet cleaners and floor waxers.</p>\n\t9. Concierges make an annual salary of $28,110.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6077078a74da0300181e19d2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"hotel reception\" height=\"1333\" width=\"1778\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Space_Cat/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 1,040</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/39-6012.00\">according to O*NET</a>: </strong>Concierges assist patrons with personal services, such as business services.</p>\n\t8. Restaurant, lounge, and coffee shop hosts and hostesses make an annual salary of $28,820.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ecfc72af0f41966f665e2da?format=jpeg\" alt=\"restaurant host hostess\" height=\"1333\" width=\"1777\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Ronnie Kaufman/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 1,300</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/35-9031.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>: Host and hostesses welcome patrons, seat them at tables or in lounge, and help ensure quality of facilities and service.</p>\n\t7. Transit and intercity bus drivers make an annual salary of $30,530.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ece7ed44dca68084706896e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"bus driver\" height=\"1335\" width=\"1780\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Monty Rakusen/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 1,000</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/53-3052.00\">according to O*NET</a>:&#160;</strong>They drive buses and may assist passengers.</p>\n\t5. Customer service representatives make an annual salary of $31,040.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5cae214f95cb1501813569a6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"customer service representative\" height=\"3478\" width=\"4637\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">DigitalVision/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 1,760</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/43-4051.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>:&#160;Customer service representatives assist customers with questions or complaints, either in person or over the phone.</p>\n\t4. Landscaping and groundskeeping workers make an annual salary of $32,280.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ce6c1fc9252e336f473a5ab?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Gardener\" height=\"617\" width=\"822\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A gardener irrigates a facility with imperial crowns on the grounds of the Brandenburg State Garden Show.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Jens Büttner/picture alliance via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 1,470</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/37-3011.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>: Landscaping and groundskeeping workers take care of lawns, plants, and trees. Their duties include sod laying, mowing, trimming, planting, and watering, along with keeping the area free of general trash and debris.</p>\n\t3. First-line supervisors of personal service and entertainment and recreation workers make an annual salary of $39,900.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5cb786934a167502974ac1f6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"hotel maid\" height=\"1333\" width=\"1777\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Joe Raedle/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 2,650</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/39-1021.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>:&#160;First-line supervisors of personal service workers coordinate personal service workers like make-up artists, caddies, or maids.</p>\n\t2. Maintenance and repair workers make an annual salary of $40,200.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d530ccacd97845aff1673f3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"amusement theme park worker\" height=\"984\" width=\"1312\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">JD Pooley/AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 2,440</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/49-9071.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>:&#160;Maintenance and repair workers make sure mechanical equipment is running smoothly. This includes pipe fitting, boiler repairs, welding, carpentry, and other general building repairs.</p>\n\t1. First-line supervisors of food preparation and serving workers make an annual salary of $41,540.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d4d6b0217e5d72a6b620774?format=jpeg\" alt=\"how much to tip waiter\" height=\"1351\" width=\"1801\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Jasper Juinen/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong>Total employed in US amusement parks and arcades:</strong> 1,240</p><p><strong>What they do, <a href=\"https://www.onetonline.org/link/summary/35-1012.00\">according to O*NET</a></strong>:&#160;First-line supervisors of food preparation and serving workers coordinate workers to ensure efficient customer service.</p>\n\tMethod and data source\n\t\n\t<p>The salaries of amusement park workers in the US vary widely. The Bureau of Labor Statistics' <a href=\"https://www.bls.gov/oes/home.htm\">Occupational Employment and Wage Statistics&#160;program</a>&#160;offers data on employment and wages across different occupations and industries.</p><p>According to BLS, the <a href=\"https://www.bls.gov/oes/current/naics4_713100.htm\">amusement parks and arcades industry</a> employed about 125,250 people in May 2020, the most recent period for which data is available. The typical annual wage for all occupations in this industry is lower than the median for all occupations regardless of industry. The median annual wage in the amusement parks and arcades industry was $27,300, far below the median across all industries of $41,950.</p><p>For our analysis, we looked at the occupations with at least 1,000 employees in the amusement parks and arcades industry in May 2020. We then ranked this set of occupations from the lowest to highest median annual wage. We excluded sales representatives of services because although they had at least 1,000 employees, no median annual salary estimate was available for May 2020.&#160;</p><p>In addition to the annual salaries, the above slides also include the number of people employed in each occupation in this industry.</p>\n</div><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a cb1501813569a6?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn85@2020_4/2021/04/14/18-15-31-503_0d82caef1235c594.webp","https://i.insider.com/5ce6c1fc9252e336f473a5ab?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn82@2020_2/2021/04/14/18-15-35-251_a1d268f01804738f.webp","https://i.insider.com/5cb786934a167502974ac1f6?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn89@2020_2/2021/04/14/18-15-32-008_423a699c783d4f67.webp","https://i.insider.com/5d530ccacd97845aff1673f3?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn93@2020_3/2021/04/14/18-15-35-199_39668ac5ea5d3793.webp","https://i.insider.com/5d4d6b0217e5d72a6b620774?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn1@2020_3/2021/04/14/18-15-30-102_9f141dbe43d135c3.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn1@2020_2/2021/04/14/18-15-35-145_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=F4nuX9TxQI0:GVnFNVJunnA:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn66@2020_1/2021/04/14/18-15-33-605_cc15823696533faf.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=F4nuX9TxQI0:GVnFNVJunnA:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn33@2020_2/2021/04/14/18-15-33-459_1b82b203c382ea32.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn29@2020_4/2021/04/14/18-15-29-996_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=F4nuX9TxQI0:GVnFNVJunnA:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn46@2020_6/2021/04/14/18-15-29-224_e0afb5c989a38cde.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/F4nuX9TxQI0":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn20@2020_4/2021/04/14/18-15-28-422_7a86751b89e7c69d.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1618424108845},{"createdTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","updatedTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:08","title":"How to add page numbers to a Microsoft Word document header or footer on a PC or Mac","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-add-page-numbers-in-word","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60761f054206150018175535?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Types on a laptop and computer\" height=\"1060\" width=\"2121\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can add customized page numbers to your Word document easily.\n<p class=\"copyright\">alvarez/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>You can add page numbers in Word to the header or footer sections of your document.</li>\n<li>Once you enable page numbers in the Insert menu, Word can automatically number all your pages.</li>\n<li>Page numbers can come in a variety of styles, sizes, and fonts.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Visit Insider&#39;s Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Adding page numbers to long Microsoft Word documents takes just a few clicks. The pages are numbered automatically, so you don&#39;t need to add them in one by one. </p><p>You can have page numbers at the top or bottom of the page, and there are a variety of styles to choose from (top-right corner, bottom-center, et cetera). </p><p>Here&#39;s how to add page numbers in Word, using either a Mac or PC. </p><h2><strong>How to add page numbers in Word on macOS</strong></h2><p><strong>1. </strong>In the Insert tab of an open document, click the Page Number icon.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6076111a74da0300181e1819?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 1\" height=\"866\" width=\"2091\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Select the Insert tab before clicking the Page Numbers button.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abbey White/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>2. </strong>Select Page Number.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6076113d74da0300181e181a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 2\" height=\"562\" width=\"1230\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Select Page Number from the dropdown menu.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abbey White/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3. </strong>Choose where you want the page numbers to appear, as well as an alignment style.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607611913e3fe7001882a7f6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 3\" height=\"1010\" width=\"1801\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Choose whether you want your page numbers in your header or footer.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abbey White/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4. </strong>Uncheck the &#34;Show number on first page&#34; box if you don&#39;t want the first page of your document to be numbered.</p><p><strong>5. </strong>If you want to choose a different numbering style, click Format and choose from the list of options.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607611b03e3fe7001882a7f7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 4\" height=\"912\" width=\"1706\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can make slight adjustments to your page number formatting.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abbey White/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>6. </strong>Once you&#39;re finished, click OK. They&#39;ll appear immediately. If you want to edit them, you can double-click them in the header or footer.</p><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><h2><strong>How to include the total number of pages in a Word document on macOS</strong></h2><p>Among the many options for customizing your page numbers is the ability to also feature the total number of pages in your Word document on macOS.</p><p>If you want a reader to be able to see what page out of the total number of document pages they&#39;re on, start by double-clicking the header or footer, depending on where you placed your page numbers. </p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607612b874da0300181e181c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 5\" height=\"1066\" width=\"2086\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Select TK as a Footer style to see the total number of pages in your Word document.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abbey White/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Then, while on the Header &#38; Footer menu, choose &#34;Footer&#34; and select the Semaphore style from the drop-down menu. When you&#39;ve finished editing, click &#34;Close Header and Footer&#34; or double-click any area outside of the header or footer to get back to your document.</p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Quick tip:</strong> You can only see the current page out of the total number of pages in the Footer, as it&#39;s not available as a Header.</p></aside></aside><h2>How to add page numbers in Word on Windows</h2><p><strong>1. </strong>In an open document, click Insert. </p><p><strong>2. </strong>Choose Page Number.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6076175d420615001817551f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 6\" height=\"482\" width=\"892\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Under the Insert tab select Page Numbers.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3. </strong>Select a location - either header or footer - for page numbers from the drop-down menu, then scroll through the style options and click the one you like best.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6076178474da0300181e1826?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 7\" height=\"661\" width=\"825\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Choose the style of page number you want for your header or footer.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4. </strong>If you don&#39;t want the first page or title page of your document numbered, go to the Design tab and choose Different First Page.</p><p><strong>5. </strong>Select Page Number followed by Format Page Numbers.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6076188074da0300181e1829?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 11\" height=\"402\" width=\"822\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Select format from the Page Number dropdown menu.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>6. </strong>Click the circle next to &#34;Start at:&#34; and set the number to zero.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607618ac4206150018175529?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 9\" height=\"502\" width=\"818\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Set the Start at value to 0 to remove page numbers of the first page of your document.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>7. </strong>Select OK before choosing Close Header and Footer to finish editing.</p><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><h2>How to include the total number of pages in a Word document on Windows</h2><p>Like Word for macOS users, Windows users with Microsoft Word can also include the total page count of their document alongside individual page numbers.</p><p>The process follows many of the same steps as inserting page numbers - going to the Insert menu, and selecting Page Number from the drop-down before choosing the location of the page numbers. </p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607619854206150018175531?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Page Numbers 10\" height=\"578\" width=\"936\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Choose the &#34;X of Y&#34; option for page number totals in Word on Windows.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The difference is that when you&#39;re scrolling through the page number formats, you&#39;ll want to locate and pick the &#34;Page X of Y&#34; section. There are multiple alignment styles for this - left, center, and right - and once you&#39;ve picked which you want, click Close Header and Footer to set it. </p></aside><bi-shortcode
